# 🚀 THE COMPLETE ESCAPE PLAN 2026 v3 (Rich Syllabus)
**Tuesday, April 21, 2026 → Thursday, December 31, 2026**

---

## 📋 Mission Briefing
1. **Focus on depth.** Build muscle memory for modern full-stack workflows.
2. **Projects > Tutorials.** The 5 major projects in this plan are your keys to employment.
3. **Consistency.** 1.5hrs daily, 4hrs weekends.

---


## ────────────────────────────────────────
## 📅 WEEK 2 (Apr 21)
## ────────────────────────────────────────

### Tuesday, Apr 21 - Day 11
**Topic:** Events & Bubbling (Phase 1: Advanced JS & DOM (April - May))
**Sessions:** 2

#### Session 1: Events & Bubbling (50 min)
**Pre-Session Questions (Answer BEFORE coding):**
1. How does the browser know a button was clicked?
2. What is Event Bubbling vs Capturing?

**Core Topics:**
- addEventListener() and event handlers
- The Event object (e.target, e.preventDefault())
- Event Bubbling (bottom-up propagation)
- Event Capturing (top-down)
- Event Delegation (attaching one listener to a parent)

**Resources:**
- [JS.info: Event Bubbling](https://javascript.info/bubbling-and-capturing)
- [MDN: Events](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/JavaScript/Building_blocks/Events)

**Code & Notes (Write during session):**

**What it is:**
[Explain in your own words]

**Why it exists & How it works:**
[Mechanism/process]

```javascript
// Implementation examples
```

**Daily Exercises ✅:**
1. [ ] **Exercise 1:** Attach a click listener to a button that logs its dataset value.
2. [ ] **Exercise 2:** Create a parent <div> with 3 child <button>s. Use Event Delegation to listen to clicks on the parent only.
3. [ ] **Exercise 3:** Use e.stopPropagation() to stop a child click from reaching the parent.

**Post-Session Recall (CLOSE EVERYTHING FIRST!):**
1. **Explain Event Delegation and why it saves memory.**
   - [Your answer from memory]
2. **What does e.preventDefault() do on a form?**
   - [Your answer from memory]
3. **Which direction does Bubbling go?**
   - [Your answer from memory]

### Saturday, Apr 25 - Day 15
**Topic:** Promises & Async/Await (Phase 1: Advanced JS & DOM (April - May))
**Sessions:** 4

#### Session 1: Promises & Async/Await (50 min)
**Pre-Session Questions (Answer BEFORE coding):**
1. What is callback hell and how do Promises solve it?
2. What is the difference between .then() and await?

**Core Topics:**
- Promise states (Pending, Fulfilled, Rejected)
- Chaining .then() and .catch()
- The async keyword and returning Promises
- Using try/catch with async/await
- Promise.all() for running tasks in parallel

**Resources:**
- [JS.info: Promises](https://javascript.info/promise-basics)
- [MDN: Async/Await](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/async_function)

**Code & Notes (Write during session):**

[Explain in your own words]

**Why it exists & How it works:**
[Mechanism/process]

```javascript

```

**Daily Exercises ✅:**
1. [ ] **Exercise 1:** Convert a callback-based setTimeout into a reusable Promise-based delay() function.
2. [ ] **Exercise 2:** Chain two API calls using .then() where the second depends on the first.
3. [ ] **Exercise 3:** Rewrite the exact same logic using async/await and try/catch block.
4. [ ] **Exercise 4:** BONUS: Trigger 3 promises simultaneously using Promise.all().

**Post-Session Recall (CLOSE EVERYTHING FIRST!):**

### Monday, Apr 27 - Day 17
**Topic:** DOM Manipulation (Phase 1: Advanced JS & DOM (April - May))
**Sessions:** 2

#### Session 1: DOM Manipulation (50 min)
**Pre-Session Questions (Answer BEFORE coding):**
1. What exactly is the Document Object Model?
2. How do you select an element vs multiple elements?

**Core Topics:**
- document.querySelector / querySelectorAll
- Updating textContent vs innerHTML
- Changing styles and classList (add, remove, toggle)
- Creating and appending elements (createElement, appendChild)
- Document fragments for performance

**Resources:**
- [JS.info: Document](https://javascript.info/document)
- [MDN: DOM Introduction](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Document_Object_Model/Introduction)

**Code & Notes (Write during session):**

**What it is:**
[Explain in your own words]

**Why it exists & How it works:**
[Mechanism/process]

```javascript
// Implementation examples
```

**Daily Exercises ✅:**
1. [ ] **Exercise 1:** Select a div and change its background color and text based on a variable.
2. [ ] **Exercise 2:** Create an unordered list <ul> and dynamically append 5 <li> elements using a loop.
3. [ ] **Exercise 3:** Toggle a 'dark-mode' class on the body when a button is clicked.

**Post-Session Recall (CLOSE EVERYTHING FIRST!):**

#### Session 1: Events & Bubbling (50 min)
**Pre-Session Questions (Answer BEFORE coding):**
1. How does the browser know a button was clicked?
2. What is Event Bubbling vs Capturing?

**Core Topics:**
- addEventListener() and event handlers
- The Event object (e.target, e.preventDefault())
- Event Bubbling (bottom-up propagation)
- Event Capturing (top-down)
- Event Delegation (attaching one listener to a parent)

- Fetching data inside useEffect

**Resources:**
- [React Docs: Synchronizing with Effects](https://react.dev/learn/synchronizing-with-effects)

**Code & Notes (Write during session):**

**What it is:**
[Explain in your own words]

**Why it exists & How it works:**
[Mechanism/process]

```javascript
// Implementation examples
```

**Daily Exercises ✅:**
1. [ ] **Exercise 1:** Fetch data from an API on component mount and save to state.
2. [ ] **Exercise 2:** Write an effect that logs whenever a specific prop changes.
3. [ ] **Exercise 3:** Write an effect that sets a setInterval, and critically, a cleanup function that clears it on unmount.

**Post-Session Recall (CLOSE EVERYTHING FIRST!):**
1. **What happens if you omit the dependency array in useEffect?**
   - [Your answer from memory]
2. **What is the cleanup function used for?**
   - [Your answer from memory]

   - [Your answer from memory]
